<p><br/></p>
<p>The following is a list of <b>notable deaths in December 2016</b>.</p>
<p>Entries for each day are listed <u>alphabetically</u> by surname. A typical entry lists information in the following sequence:</p>
<ul>
<li>Name, age, country of citizenship at birth, subsequent country of citizenship (if applicable), reason for notability, cause of death (if known), and reference.</li>
</ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="December_2016">December 2016</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Deaths_in_December_2016&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: December 2016">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1">1</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Deaths_in_December_2016&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: 1">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Sulabha_Brahme" title="Sulabha Brahme">Sulabha Brahme</a>, 84, Indian economist.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Don_Calfa" title="Don Calfa">Don Calfa</a>, 76, American actor (<i><a href="/wiki/The_Return_of_the_Living_Dead" title="The Return of the Living Dead">The Return of the Living Dead</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Weekend_at_Bernie%27s" title="Weekend at Bernie's">Weekend at Bernie's</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Me,_Myself_and_I_(film)" title="Me, Myself and I (film)">Me, Myself and I</a></i>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Elisabeth_Carron" title="Elisabeth Carron">Elisabeth Carron</a>, 94, American operatic soprano.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jacques_Cohen_(actor)" title="Jacques Cohen (actor)">Jacques Cohen</a>, 86, Egyptian-born Israeli actor (<i><a href="/wiki/HaMis%27ada_HaGdola" title="HaMis'ada HaGdola">HaMis'ada HaGdola</a></i>), complications from pneumonia.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Peter_Corrigan" title="Peter Corrigan">Peter Corrigan</a>, 75, Australian architect.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/G%C3%A9rard_Desrosiers" title="Gérard Desrosiers">Gérard Desrosiers</a>, 97, Canadian physician.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6"><a href="#cite_note-6">[6]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jo-Anna_Downey" title="Jo-Anna Downey">Jo-Anna Downey</a>, 50, Canadian comedian, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ALS" title="ALS">ALS</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7"><a href="#cite_note-7">[7]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Inkulab" title="Inkulab">Inkulab</a>, 72, Indian poet and political activist.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Barry_Lloyd_(cricketer)" title="Barry Lloyd (cricketer)">Barry Lloyd</a>, 63, Welsh cricketer (<a href="/wiki/Glamorgan_County_Cricket_Club" title="Glamorgan County Cricket Club">Glamorgan</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9"><a href="#cite_note-9">[9]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Joe_McKnight" title="Joe McKnight">Joe McKnight</a>, 28, American football player (<a href="/wiki/New_York_Jets" title="New York Jets">New York Jets</a>), shot.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10"><a href="#cite_note-10">[10]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ljubo_Sirc" title="Ljubo Sirc">Ljubo Sirc</a>, 96, Slovene economist.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11"><a href="#cite_note-11">[11]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ousmane_Sow" title="Ousmane Sow">Ousmane Sow</a>, 81, Senegalese sculptor.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12"><a href="#cite_note-12">[12]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Zekarias_Yohannes" title="Zekarias Yohannes">Zekarias Yohannes</a>, 91, Eritrean <a href="/wiki/Eritrean_Catholic_Church" title="Eritrean Catholic Church">Catholic</a> hierarch, Bishop of <a href="/wiki/Eritrean_Catholic_Archeparchy_of_Asmara" title="Eritrean Catholic Archeparchy of Asmara">Asmara</a> (1984–2001).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13"><a href="#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2">2</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Deaths_in_December_2016&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: 2">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Odeefuo_Boa_Amponsem_III" title="Odeefuo Boa Amponsem III">Odeefuo Boa Amponsem III</a>, 94, Ghanaian royal, King of <a href="/wiki/Denkyira" title="Denkyira">Denkyira</a> (since 1955).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14"><a href="#cite_note-14">[14]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Coral_Atkins" title="Coral Atkins">Coral Atkins</a>, 80, English actress (<i><a href="/wiki/A_Family_at_War" title="A Family at War">A Family at War</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Emmerdale" title="Emmerdale">Emmerdale</a></i>), cancer.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15"><a href="#cite_note-15">[15]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Lyle_Bouck" title="Lyle Bouck">Lyle Bouck</a>, 92, American military officer and war veteran (<a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Bulge" title="Battle of the Bulge">Battle of the Bulge</a>), pneumonia.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16"><a href="#cite_note-16">[16]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/H._Keith_H._Brodie" title="H. Keith H. Brodie">H. Keith H. Brodie</a>, 77, American psychiatrist and educator, President of <a href="/wiki/Duke_University" title="Duke University">Duke University</a> (1985–1993).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-17"><a href="#cite_note-17">[17]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Joan_Chalmers" title="Joan Chalmers">Joan Chalmers</a>, 88, Canadian philanthropist.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18"><a href="#cite_note-18">[18]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Billy_Chapin" title="Billy Chapin">Billy Chapin</a>, 72, American child actor (<i><a href="/wiki/The_Night_of_the_Hunter_(film)" title="The Night of the Hunter (film)">The Night of the Hunter</a></i>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-19"><a href="#cite_note-19">[19]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Paul_de_Wispelaere" title="Paul de Wispelaere">Paul de Wispelaere</a>, 88, Belgian writer.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20"><a href="#cite_note-20">[20]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Dejo_Fayemi" title="Dejo Fayemi">Dejo Fayemi</a>, 83, Nigerian footballer (<a href="/wiki/Nigeria_national_football_team" title="Nigeria national football team">national team</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-21"><a href="#cite_note-21">[21]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Mark_Gray_(singer)" title="Mark Gray (singer)">Mark Gray</a>, 64, American country singer and songwriter (<i><a href="/wiki/Take_Me_Down" title="Take Me Down">Take Me Down</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/The_Closer_You_Get_(song)" title="The Closer You Get (song)">The Closer You Get</a></i>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-22"><a href="#cite_note-22">[22]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Halvar_Jonson" title="Halvar Jonson">Halvar Jonson</a>, 75, Canadian politician, Alberta MLA (1982–2004).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-23"><a href="#cite_note-23">[23]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Sammy_Lee_(diver)" title="Sammy Lee (diver)">Sammy Lee</a>, 96, American diver, Olympic champion (<a href="/wiki/Diving_at_the_1948_Summer_Olympics" title="Diving at the 1948 Summer Olympics">1948</a>, <a href="/wiki/Diving_at_the_1952_Summer_Olympics" title="Diving at the 1952 Summer Olympics">1952</a>), pneumonia.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-24"><a href="#cite_note-24">[24]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ko._Si._Mani" title="Ko. Si. Mani">Ko. Si. Mani</a>, 87, Indian politician.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-25"><a href="#cite_note-25">[25]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Gisela_May" title="Gisela May">Gisela May</a>, 92, German actress and singer (<a href="/wiki/Berliner_Ensemble" title="Berliner Ensemble">Berliner Ensemble</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-26"><a href="#cite_note-26">[26]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/James_Reiss" title="James Reiss">James Reiss</a>, 75, American poet and novelist.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-27"><a href="#cite_note-27">[27]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Teri_Rofkar" title="Teri Rofkar">Teri Rofkar</a>, 60, American <a href="/wiki/Tlingit" title="Tlingit">Tlingit</a> weaver.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-28"><a href="#cite_note-28">[28]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Rocco_Salini" title="Rocco Salini">Rocco Salini</a>, 85, Italian politician, <a href="/wiki/List_of_Presidents_of_Abruzzo" title="List of Presidents of Abruzzo">President of Abruzzo</a> (1990–1992).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-29"><a href="#cite_note-29">[29]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jean_Stead" title="Jean Stead">Jean Stead</a>, 90, British journalist (<i><a href="/wiki/The_Guardian" title="The Guardian">The Guardian</a></i>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-30"><a href="#cite_note-30">[30]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bosco_Tjan" title="Bosco Tjan">Bosco Tjan</a>, 50, American professor and psychologist, stabbed.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-31"><a href="#cite_note-31">[31]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Tove_Kari_Viken" title="Tove Kari Viken">Tove Kari Viken</a>, 74, Norwegian politician, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Member_of_Parliament#Norway" title="Member of Parliament">MP</a> (1989–1997).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-32"><a href="#cite_note-32">[32]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="3">3</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Deaths_in_December_2016&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: 3">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Rustam_Asildarov" title="Rustam Asildarov">Rustam Asildarov</a>, 35, Russian militant leader (<a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">ISIS</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-33"><a href="#cite_note-33">[33]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Willie_Casey_(Gaelic_footballer)" title="Willie Casey (Gaelic footballer)">Willie Casey</a>, 84, Irish Gaelic football player (<a href="/wiki/Mayo_GAA" title="Mayo GAA">Mayo</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-34"><a href="#cite_note-34">[34]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Newman_Darby" title="Newman Darby">Newman Darby</a>, 88, American inventor (<a href="/wiki/Windsurfing" title="Windsurfing">sailboard</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-35"><a href="#cite_note-35">[35]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Gigliola_Frazzoni" title="Gigliola Frazzoni">Gigliola Frazzoni</a>, 93, Italian opera singer.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-36"><a href="#cite_note-36">[36]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nikola_Gigov" title="Nikola Gigov">Nikola Gigov</a>, 79, Bulgarian author.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-37"><a href="#cite_note-37">[37]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Herbert_Hardesty" title="Herbert Hardesty">Herbert Hardesty</a>, 91, American jazz musician.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-38"><a href="#cite_note-38">[38]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/David_Hay_(cardiologist)" title="David Hay (cardiologist)">Sir David Hay</a>, 88, New Zealand cardiologist, anti-smoking campaigner.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-39"><a href="#cite_note-39">[39]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Arthur_Latham" title="Arthur Latham">Arthur Latham</a>, 86, British politician, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Member_of_Parliament#United_Kingdom" title="Member of Parliament">MP</a> for <a href="/wiki/Paddington_North_(UK_Parliament_constituency)" title="Paddington North (UK Parliament constituency)">Paddington North</a> (1969–1974) and <a href="/wiki/Paddington_(UK_Parliament_constituency)" title="Paddington (UK Parliament constituency)">Paddington</a> (1974–1979), Leader of <a href="/wiki/London_Borough_of_Havering" title="London Borough of Havering">London Borough of Havering</a> (1990–1996).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-40"><a href="#cite_note-40">[40]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bengt_Lindqvist" title="Bengt Lindqvist">Bengt Lindqvist</a>, 80, Swedish politician, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Riksdagen" title="Riksdagen">MP</a> (1982–1995).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-41"><a href="#cite_note-41">[41]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bhai_Mahavir" title="Bhai Mahavir">Bhai Mahavir</a>, 94, Indian politician, Governor of <a href="/wiki/Madhya_Pradesh" title="Madhya Pradesh">Madhya Pradesh</a> (1998-2003).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42"><a href="#cite_note-42">[42]</a></sup></li>

<li><a href="/wiki/Raj_Brar" title="Raj Brar">Raj Brar</a>, 44, Indian singer and actor.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-552"><a href="#cite_note-552">[552]</a></sup></li>

<li><a href="/wiki/Henning_Christophersen" title="Henning Christophersen">Henning Christophersen</a>, 77, Danish politician, <a href="/wiki/List_of_Foreign_ministers_of_Denmark" title="List of Foreign ministers of Denmark">Foreign Minister</a> (1978–1979), <a href="/wiki/List_of_Finance_Ministers_of_Denmark" title="List of Finance Ministers of Denmark">Finance Minister</a> (1982–1984), <a href="/wiki/Vice-President_of_the_European_Commission" title="Vice-President of the European Commission">Vice-President of the European Commission</a> (1985–1995).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-555"><a href="#cite_note-555">[555]</a></sup></li>
